>>> SCRIPT CONTENT <<<
-- Developer: Jessie
-- Ticket: SUP-138635
-- Purpose: Select member bank currently have DA bank enabled
-- Last modified by: SUP-138635_IT_Jessie
-- Last modified date: 2026-05-03 16:30:00

select mb.member_id as member_id, m.code as merchant_code, b.id as bank_id
from `CashMarket`.`member_bank` mb
         inner join `CashMarket`.`bank` b on b.id = mb.bank_id
         inner join `CashMarket`.`merchant` m on m.id = mb.merchant_id
 where b.code = 'DAB'
 and mb.status = 'A';
>>> END CONTENT <<<
